                        <div data-reactid="396">
                         Immerse yourself in the sanctuary that is Casa Susalito's! Located on top of a hill , midway between the glitter of LA county, beaches from Malibu north and the laid back vibe of Santa Barbara, Ventura and Ojai. A place to relax and refresh.
                        </div>
                        <div data-reactid="397">
                         Immerse yourself in the sanctuary that is Casa Susalito's! Located on top of a hill with a view of the Conejo Valley, plan on a restful, beautiful house to return to after a day of adventure. In Thousand Oaks, Midway between the glitter of LA county, with its many attractions including Universal Studios, the beaches of highway one, including Malibu and Zuma, and the laid back vibe of Ventura, Ojai and Santa Barbara, you will be able to return at the end of your day and kick back, feel the sun on your face, lounge in the seasonal pool, or sit by the fire pit in the evening and enjoy some s'mores and stars. Casa Susalito's is set up to encourage outdoor living, with a seasonal pool, lounge chairs, picnic table, BBQ, firepit and plantings that attract birds and butterflies, and yet also has a cozy fireplace for when the weather is inclement. Cook on a real reconditioned Merritt O'Keefe stove, with that pancake griddle you remember from your grandmother's house. And each bedroom is themed...The Impressionism room, and the Hawaiian room, so you have the feeling of truly getting away from it all. All in all, a vacation home to return to again and again.
                        </div>
                        <div data-reactid="398">
                         If you like Yo walk, you can stroll down to the nearby Whole Foods for gourmet goodies. Peet's coffee is close by as well.
                        </div>

                        <div data-reactid="992">
                         <li data-reactid="993"><p data-reactid="994">Brett Sabre is very nice and friendly. I had lived there for 21 days. I had a good memory with him. </p><span data-reactid="995">是青</span><span data-reactid="996">2016-09-22T00:00:00Z</span></li>
                         <li data-reactid="997"><p data-reactid="998">I stayed 2 nights at Brett's home. I was looking for something simple and on a budget and this pretty much did the trick. It was 10 min from the 101 and there is a Vons, Starbucks, and a few stores about a 5 minute drive down Rt 23. The neighborhood was like a maze so I was happy to have gps. The listing is very honest and nothing is hidden. You do have to bring your own blankets/pillow though and the kitchen is definitely out for use unless u wanna store a drink in there. There is a rack for clothes but no hangers and a window which u can open/close at night bc it does get warm/chilly. Target is 10 min North on the 101 in case u need stuff. He does require you have a legal photo ID for record purposes as he scans it in the computer when you check in. The neighbors do have dogs and a rooster that crows all day. So if you are a light sleeper or hate such sounds you should rethink your booking decision. I honestly didn't care about the noise. Brett does smoke an occassional pipe so that could bother people I guess. My car was safe to park on the street and Brett's cats pretty much kept to themselves. But if u hate animals or have an allergy this wouldn't be the place for you. Overall, Brett was pretty much a relaxed host and very accomodating. He doesn't run a 5 Star so if you are not picky and won't fret over appearance or amenities you can def book here.</p><span data-reactid="999">Jackie</span><span data-reactid="1000">2016-07-06T00:00:00Z</span></li>

I would only recommend this place for someone who doesn't need to extensively use the kitchen. That's perfectly understandable though as kitchen use is not advertised. </p><span data-reactid="1007">Karthik</span><span data-reactid="1008">2016-08-06T00:00:00Z</span></li>

                         <li data-reactid="1013"><p data-reactid="1014">If you are looking for a cheap room to rent then this would be for you. If you're looking for comfort and homey feel this probably isn't for you. He does have a small air mattress for the room but does not have linens. He however does not advertise that he does and when I asked him he gladly lent me a comforter. Brett was very friendly and welcoming. I have stayed in other Air bnb's in the area for only about $10/night and got much more.</p><span data-reactid="1015">Ashley</span><span data-reactid="1016">2016-06-12T00:00:00Z</span></li>
